# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've completed the comprehensive analysis of the HTTP filter chain extension mechanism in Envoy v1.31.2. Here's what I found:

## Summary

The HTTP filter chain extension architecture consists of **13 key C++ source files** and **22 core symbols** that work together:

### Core Components:

1. **Interface Layer** (`envoy/http/filter_factory.h` & `filter.h`):
   - `FilterFactoryCb`: The callback type for creating filters
   - `FilterContext`: Metadata passed during filter chain creation
   - `FilterChainManager`: Interface for applying filter factories
   - `StreamFilterBase`, `StreamDecoderFilter`, `StreamEncoderFilter`: Filter types

2. **Factory Registry** (`envoy/server/filter_config.h`):
   - `NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Interface for registering downstream filters
   - `UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory`: Interface for upstream filters
   - `HttpFilterConfigFactoryBase`: Common factory base with metadata support

3. **Template Helpers** (`source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h`):
   - `FactoryBase`: Template base reducing boilerplate for filter factory implementations
   - `CommonFactoryBase`: Handles protobuf message and route config creation
   - `DualFactoryBase`: Supports both downstream and upstream filters

4. **Runtime Execution** (`source/common/http/filter_manager.h/cc`):
   - `FilterManager`: Manages per-stream filter chains
   - `ActiveStreamFilterBase`: Wrapper tracking iteration state for each filter
   - `FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl`: Implementation of the callbacks interface

5. **Dynamic Discovery** (`source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h`):
   - `DynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl`: Manages ECDS configuration updates
   - `HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl`: HTTP-specific dynamic filter provider
   - `NamedHttpFilte

Filter Base Classes (envoy/http/filter.h)\\nDefines the filter types that can be registered:\\n- **StreamFilterBase**: Base class for all HTTP filters with lifecycle management (onDestroy, onStreamComplete).\\n- **StreamDecoderFilter**: Processes request headers, data, and trailers flowing downstream.\\n- **StreamEncoderFilter**: Processes response headers, data, and trailers flowing upstream.\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacks**: Interface used by filters to register themselves in a chain (addStreamDecoderFilter, addStreamEncoderFilter, addStreamFilter).\\n\\n## 3. Method `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` returns FilterFactoryCb.\\n- **UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Similar to NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory but for upstream (to-cluster) filters.\\n\\n## 4. Template Factory Base (source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h)\\nProvides boilerplate reduction:\\n- **CommonFactoryBase**: Template base with protobuf message handling and route config support.\\n- **FactoryBase**: Inherits from CommonFactoryBase and NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory, implementing createFilterFactoryFromProto() that calls the pure virtual createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped().\\n- **DualFactoryBase**: Supports both downstream and upstream by inheriting from both NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory and UpstreamHttpFilterConfigFactory.\\n\\n## 5. Per-Request Filter Chain Execution (source/common/http/filter_manager.h and filter_manager.cc)\\nManages the actual runtime filter chain for each stream:\\n- **FilterManager**: Main class managing filter chains for a connection. Contains the stream state, filters lists, and iteration logic.\\n- **ActiveStreamFilterBase**: Wrapper around each filter instance tracking:\\n  - Iteration state (Continue, StopIteration, etc.)\\n  - Whether it's encoder or decoder (or both)\\n  - FilterContext metadata\\n  - Methods like commonContinue() to resume iteration after async operations\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl**: Implementation of FilterChainFactoryCallbacks that adds decoded/encoded/stream filters to the FilterManager's lists.\\n- The execution chain is a bidirectional list of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter objects that are iterated through.\\n\\n## 6. Filter Chain Construction (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h and filter_chain_helper.cc)\\nOrchestrates filter chain assembly from configuration:\\n- **FilterChainUtility**: Static methods for:\\n  - createFilterChainForFactories(): Iterates through FilterFactoriesList and calls applyFilterFactoryCb for each.\\n  - Singleton factory management for downstream/upstream filter config providers.\\n- **FilterChainHelper**: Template class that processes filter configuration protos to build FilterFactoriesList, handling both static and dynamic (ECDS) filters. The processFilters() method validates dependencies and creates filter config providers.\\n\\n## 8. Filter Manager Implementation (source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h and filter_chain_manager_impl.cc)\\nImplements FilterChainManager interface:\\n- **FilterChainManagerImpl**: Manages network-level filter chains with support for hot reloading and multi-address listeners.\\n\\n## Execution Flow:\\n1. **Configuration Time**: FilterChainHelper processes HttpFilter protos, looking up NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory for each filter, calling createFilterFactoryFromProto() to get FilterFactoryCb, and storing in FilterFactoriesList.\\n2. **Stream Creation**: When a new HTTP stream is created, FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories() iterates the list and calls FilterChainManager::applyFilterFactoryCb().\\n3. **Filter Instantiation**: applyFilterFactoryCb() creates FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl and invokes the FilterFactoryCb, which calls addStreamDecoderFilter/addStreamEncoderFilter/addStreamFilter on the callbacks.\\n4. **Filter Execution**: FilterManager maintains lists of ActiveStreamDecoderFilter and ActiveStreamEncoderFilter, iterating through them as data flows (headers, data, trailers) bidirectionally. The commonContinue() methods in ActiveStreamFilterBase handle resumption after filters return StopIteration or async operations complete.\\n5. **Dynamic Updates**: HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl listens for ECDS updates, instantiates new filter factories on config change, and updates thread-local storage atomically across worker threads.\\n\\nThe architecture separates concerns cleanly: interface definitions (filter.h, filter_factory.h) from factory registration (filter_config.h), template helpers (factory_base.h), and runtime execution (filter_manager.h/cc).\"\n}\n",
